    "code": 'import os\nimport json\nimport requests\nfrom datetime import datetime\nimport subprocess\nimport time\n\nprint("=== NATIONAL GEOGRAPHIC FIRST YOUTUBE VIDEO RESEARCH (PHASE 2) ===\\n")\nprint("Objective: Find the first National Geographic short video on YouTube")\nprint("Strategy: Use SerpApi + targeted yt-dlp searches to avoid timeout\\n")\n\n# Create workspace directory\nworkspace_dir = "workspace"\nos.makedirs(workspace_dir, exist_ok=True)\nprint(f"Workspace directory: {workspace_dir}")\n\n# Step 1: Check if we have previous research data\nprint("\\n=== STEP 1: CHECKING PREVIOUS RESEARCH DATA ===\\n")\n\nprevious_summary = None\nsummary_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'ng_research_summary.json\')\nif os.path.exists(summary_file):\n    print(f"Found previous research summary: {summary_file}")\n    with open(summary_file, \'r\') as f:\n        previous_summary = json.load(f)\n    print("Previous research completed - proceeding with targeted searches")\nelse:\n    print("No previous research found - starting fresh")\n\n# Step 2: Use SerpApi to search for National Geographic\'s earliest YouTube content\nprint("\\n=== STEP 2: SERPAPI SEARCH FOR EARLIEST NG CONTENT ===\\n")\n\nserpapi_key = os.environ.get(\'SERPAPI_API_KEY\')\nif serpapi_key:\n    print(f"SerpApi key available: {serpapi_key[:10]}...")\n    \n    # Multiple targeted search queries\n    search_queries = [\n        "National Geographic YouTube 2006 first video",\n        "National Geographic oldest YouTube upload", \n        "site:youtube.com/channel/UCpVm7bg6pXKo1Pr6k5kxG9A oldest",\n        "National Geographic YouTube channel history first",\n        "National Geographic short film #9 YouTube"\n    ]\n    \n    serpapi_results = []\n    \n    for i, query in enumerate(search_queries):\n        print(f"Search {i+1}: \'{query}\'")\n        \n        try:\n            # SerpApi Google search\n            params = {\n                \'engine\': \'google\',\n                \'q\': query,\n                \'api_key\': serpapi_key,\n                \'num\': 10\n            }\n            \n            response = requests.get(\'https://serpapi.com/search\', params=params, timeout=30)\n            \n            if response.status_code == 200:\n                data = response.json()\n                organic_results = data.get(\'organic_results\', [])\n                \n                print(f"  Found {len(organic_results)} results")\n                \n                # Filter for YouTube results\n                youtube_results = []\n                for result in organic_results:\n                    link = result.get(\'link\', \'\')\n                    title = result.get(\'title\', \'\')\n                    snippet = result.get(\'snippet\', \'\')\n                    \n                    if \'youtube.com/watch\' in link:\n                        youtube_results.append({\n                            \'title\': title,\n                            \'link\': link,\n                            \'snippet\': snippet,\n                            \'search_query\': query\n                        })\n                        print(f"    YouTube: {title[:60]}...")\n                        print(f"             {link}")\n                \n                serpapi_results.extend(youtube_results)\n                \n            else:\n                print(f"  Error: HTTP {response.status_code}")\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"  Search failed: {str(e)}")\n        \n        # Small delay between searches\n        time.sleep(1)\n    \n    # Save SerpApi results\n    if serpapi_results:\n        serpapi_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'serpapi_ng_results.json\')\n        with open(serpapi_file, \'w\') as f:\n            json.dump(serpapi_results, f, indent=2)\n        print(f"\\nSerpApi results saved to: {serpapi_file}")\n        print(f"Total YouTube videos found: {len(serpapi_results)}")\n    \nelse:\n    print("No SerpApi key available - skipping SerpApi searches")\n\n# Step 3: Targeted yt-dlp approach - search for specific early videos\nprint("\\n=== STEP 3: TARGETED YT-DLP SEARCHES ===\\n")\n\n# Instead of downloading entire channel, search for specific patterns\nearly_video_searches = [\n    "ytsearch10:National Geographic 2006",\n    "ytsearch10:National Geographic 2007 first", \n    "ytsearch5:National Geographic oldest YouTube",\n    "ytsearch5:National Geographic #9"\n]\n\nall_early_videos = []\n\nfor search_term in early_video_searches:\n    print(f"Searching: {search_term}")\n    \n    try:\n        # Use yt-dlp to search YouTube\n        search_cmd = [\n            \'yt-dlp\',\n            \'--dump-json\',\n            \'--flat-playlist\',\n            search_term\n        ]\n        \n        result = subprocess.run(search_cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=60)\n        \n        if result.returncode == 0:\n            # Parse results\n            videos = []\n            for line in result.stdout.strip().split(\'\\n\'):\n                if line.strip():\n                    try:\n                        video_data = json.loads(line)\n                        videos.append(video_data)\n                    except json.JSONDecodeError:\n                        continue\n            \n            print(f"  Found {len(videos)} videos")\n            \n            # Show video details\n            for video in videos:\n                title = video.get(\'title\', \'Unknown\')\n                video_id = video.get(\'id\', \'Unknown\')\n                uploader = video.get(\'uploader\', \'Unknown\')\n                \n                # Check if it\'s from National Geographic\n                if \'National Geographic\' in uploader or \'NatGeo\' in uploader:\n                    print(f"    NG Video: {title[:50]}...")\n                    print(f"             ID: {video_id}")\n                    print(f"             Uploader: {uploader}")\n                    all_early_videos.append(video)\n            \n        else:\n            print(f"  Search failed: {result.stderr}")\n            \n    except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:\n        print(f"  Search timed out")\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"  Error: {str(e)}")\n\n# Step 4: Try to get specific video details for promising candidates\nprint("\\n=== STEP 4: ANALYZING CANDIDATE VIDEOS ===\\n")\n\n# Combine results from SerpApi and yt-dlp searches\ncandidate_videos = []\n\n# Extract video IDs from SerpApi results\nif \'serpapi_results\' in locals():\n    for result in serpapi_results:\n        link = result.get(\'link\', \'\')\n        if \'youtube.com/watch?v=\' in link:\n            video_id = link.split(\'watch?v=\')[1].split(\'&\')[0]\n            candidate_videos.append({\n                \'video_id\': video_id,\n                \'title\': result.get(\'title\', \'\'),\n                \'source\': \'serpapi\',\n                \'url\': link\n            })\n\n# Add yt-dlp search results\nfor video in all_early_videos:\n    candidate_videos.append({\n        \'video_id\': video.get(\'id\', \'\'),\n        \'title\': video.get(\'title\', \'\'),\n        \'source\': \'yt-dlp_search\',\n        \'uploader\': video.get(\'uploader\', \'\')\n    })\n\nprint(f"Total candidate videos to analyze: {len(candidate_videos)}")\n\n# Get detailed info for each candidate\ndetailed_videos = []\n\nfor i, candidate in enumerate(candidate_videos[:10]):  # Limit to first 10 to avoid timeout\n    video_id = candidate[\'video_id\']\n    print(f"\\nAnalyzing video {i+1}: {candidate[\'title\'][:40]}...")\n    print(f"Video ID: {video_id}")\n    \n    try:\n        # Get detailed video information\n        info_cmd = [\n            \'yt-dlp\',\n            \'--dump-json\',\n            \'--no-playlist\',\n            f\'https://www.youtube.com/watch?v={video_id}\'\n        ]\n        \n        result = subprocess.run(info_cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30)\n        \n        if result.returncode == 0:\n            video_info = json.loads(result.stdout)\n            \n            title = video_info.get(\'title\', \'Unknown\')\n            upload_date = video_info.get(\'upload_date\', \'Unknown\')\n            uploader = video_info.get(\'uploader\', \'Unknown\')\n            duration = video_info.get(\'duration\', 0)\n            description = video_info.get(\'description\', \'\')\n            \n            # Check if this is from National Geographic\n            if \'National Geographic\' in uploader or \'NatGeo\' in uploader:\n                \n                # Format upload date\n                formatted_date = \'Unknown\'\n                if upload_date and upload_date != \'Unknown\':\n                    try:\n                        date_obj = datetime.strptime(upload_date, \'%Y%m%d\')\n                        formatted_date = date_obj.strftime(\'%Y-%m-%d\')\n                    except:\n                        formatted_date = upload_date\n                \n                # Check if it\'s a short video (under 10 minutes)\n                is_short = duration and duration < 600\n                \n                # Check for \'#9\' in title or description\n                has_number_9 = \'#9\' in title or \'#9\' in description or \' 9 \' in title\n                \n                video_details = {\n                    \'video_id\': video_id,\n                    \'title\': title,\n                    \'upload_date\': upload_date,\n                    \'formatted_date\': formatted_date,\n                    \'uploader\': uploader,\n                    \'duration\': duration,\n                    \'is_short\': is_short,\n                    \'has_number_9\': has_number_9,\n                    \'description_preview\': description[:200] if description else \'\',\n                    \'url\': f\'https://www.youtube.com/watch?v={video_id}\'\n                }\n                \n                detailed_videos.append(video_details)\n                \n                print(f"  âœ“ National Geographic video confirmed")\n                print(f"    Upload Date: {formatted_date}")\n                print(f"    Duration: {duration}s ({duration//60}:{duration%60:02d})")\n                print(f"    Short video: {\'Yes\' if is_short else \'No\'}")\n                print(f"    Contains \'#9\': {\'Yes\' if has_number_9 else \'No\'}")\n                \n                if has_number_9:\n                    print(f"    *** POTENTIAL MATCH: Contains \'#9\' reference ***")\n            \n        else:\n            print(f"  Failed to get video info: {result.stderr}")\n            \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"  Error analyzing video: {str(e)}")\n\n# Step 5: Sort and identify the earliest short video\nprint("\\n=== STEP 5: IDENTIFYING EARLIEST SHORT VIDEO ===\\n")\n\nif detailed_videos:\n    # Sort by upload date\n    valid_dated_videos = [v for v in detailed_videos if v[\'upload_date\'] != \'Unknown\']\n    \n    if valid_dated_videos:\n        sorted_videos = sorted(valid_dated_videos, key=lambda x: x[\'upload_date\'])\n        \n        print("National Geographic videos found (sorted by date):")\n        \n        for i, video in enumerate(sorted_videos):\n            print(f"\\n{i+1}. {video[\'title\']}")\n            print(f"   Date: {video[\'formatted_date\']}")\n            print(f"   Duration: {video[\'duration\']}s")\n            print(f"   Short: {\'Yes\' if video[\'is_short\'] else \'No\'}")\n            print(f"   Has #9: {\'Yes\' if video[\'has_number_9\'] else \'No\'}")\n            print(f"   URL: {video[\'url\']}")\n        \n        # Find earliest short video\n        short_videos = [v for v in sorted_videos if v[\'is_short\']]\n        \n        if short_videos:\n            earliest_short = short_videos[0]\n            print(f"\\n*** EARLIEST SHORT VIDEO FOUND ***")\n            print(f"Title: {earliest_short[\'title\']}")\n            print(f"Date: {earliest_short[\'formatted_date\']}")\n            print(f"Duration: {earliest_short[\'duration\']}s")\n            print(f"Contains \'#9\': {\'Yes\' if earliest_short[\'has_number_9\'] else \'No\'}")\n            print(f"URL: {earliest_short[\'url\']}")\n            \n            if earliest_short[\'has_number_9\']:\n                print(f"\\nðŸŽ¯ SUCCESS: Found early NG short video with \'#9\' reference!")\n            else:\n                print(f"\\nâš ï¸  Note: Earliest short video doesn\'t contain \'#9\' - may need broader search")\n        \n        # Save detailed results\n        results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'ng_detailed_video_analysis.json\')\n        with open(results_file, \'w\') as f:\n            json.dump({\n                \'search_timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n                \'total_candidates_analyzed\': len(candidate_videos),\n                \'national_geographic_videos_found\': len(detailed_videos),\n                \'videos_with_dates\': len(valid_dated_videos),\n                \'short_videos_found\': len(short_videos),\n                \'earliest_short_video\': earliest_short if short_videos else None,\n                \'all_videos\': sorted_videos\n            }, f, indent=2)\n        \n        print(f"\\nDetailed analysis saved to: {results_file}")\n    \n    else:\n        print("No videos with valid dates found")\nelse:\n    print("No National Geographic videos found in search results")\n\n# List all workspace files\nprint("\\n=== WORKSPACE CONTENTS ===\\n")\nfor file in os.listdir(workspace_dir):\n    full_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file)\n    if os.path.isfile(full_path):\n        size_kb = os.path.getsize(full_path) / 1024\n        print(f"  - {file} ({size_kb:.1f} KB)")\n\nprint("\\n*** TARGETED SEARCH PHASE COMPLETE ***")\nprint("Next: If \'#9\' reference found, analyze specific video content")\nprint("If not found, may need to search National Geographic\'s actual oldest uploads")',
